<div style="text-align:center"><div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
 <p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;2.02. Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&#160;23, 2024, HCA Healthcare, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing, among other matters, its results of operations for the second quarter ended June&#160;30, 2024, the text of which is set forth as <span style="text-decoration:underline">Exhibit&#160;99.1.</span> </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;7.01. Regulation FD Disclosure. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&#160;23, 2024, the Company issued a press release announcing, among other matters, its results of operations for the second quarter ended June&#160;30, 2024, the text of which is set forth as <span style="text-decoration:underline">Exhibit&#160;99.1</span>. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;8.01. Other Events. </p> <p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&#160;23, 2024, the Company announced that its Board of Directors had declared a quarterly cash dividend of $0.66 per share of the Company&#8217;s common stock. The dividend will be paid on September&#160;30, 2024 to stockholders of record at the close of business on September&#160;16, 2024. </p> <p style="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;9.01. Financial Statements and Exhibits. </p> <p style="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>HCA HEALTHCARE REPORTS SECOND QUARTER 2024 RESULTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:16pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>RAISES 2024 GUIDANCE </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Nashville, Tenn.,
July</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;23, 2024 &#150; </B><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>HCA Healthcare, Inc</U></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. (NYSE: HCA) today announced financial and operating results for the second
quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2024. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Key second quarter metrics </B>(all percentage changes compare 2Q 2024 to 2Q 2023 unless otherwise noted): </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT><I></I><I></I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt"><I>Revenues totaled $17.492&nbsp;billion </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT><I></I><I></I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt"><I>Net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc. totaled $1.461&nbsp;billion, or $5.53 per diluted share
</I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT><I></I><I></I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt"><I>Adjusted EBITDA totaled $3.550&nbsp;billion </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT><I></I><I></I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt"><I>Cash flows from operating activities totaled $1.971&nbsp;billion </I></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><I></I><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT><I></I><I></I></TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt"><I>Same facility admissions increased 5.8&nbsp;percent while same facility equivalent admissions increased 5.2&nbsp;percent
</I></P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;The company&#146;s results for the second quarter were positive and reflected strong demand for our services. Our teams continued to
execute our strategic plan effectively and produce positive outcomes for our patients. I want to thank our HCA colleagues for their outstanding work and their continued pursuits to innovate and deliver on our mission,&#148; said Sam Hazen, Chief
Executive Officer of HCA Healthcare. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Revenues in the second quarter of 2024 totaled $17.492&nbsp;billion, compared to $15.861&nbsp;billion in the second quarter of
2023. Net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc. totaled $1.461&nbsp;billion, or $5.53 per diluted share, compared to $1.193&nbsp;billion, or $4.29 per diluted share, in the second quarter of 2023. Results for the second quarter of 2024 include
gains on sales of facilities of $12&nbsp;million, or $0.03 per diluted share. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">For the second quarter of 2024, Adjusted EBITDA totaled $3.550&nbsp;billion, compared
to $3.056&nbsp;billion in the second quarter of 2023. Adjusted EBITDA is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. A table providing supplemental information on Adjusted EBITDA and reconciling net income attributable to
HCA Healthcare, Inc. to Adjusted EBITDA is included in this release. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">1 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Same facility admissions increased 5.8&nbsp;percent while same facility equivalent admissions increased
5.2&nbsp;percent in the second quarter of 2024, compared to the prior year period. Same facility emergency room visits increased 5.5&nbsp;percent in the second quarter of 2024, compared to the prior year period. Same facility inpatient surgeries
increased 2.6&nbsp;percent, and same facility outpatient surgeries declined 2.1&nbsp;percent in the second quarter of 2024, compared to the same period of 2023. Same facility revenue per equivalent admission increased 4.4&nbsp;percent in the second
quarter of 2024, compared to the second quarter of 2023. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Six Months Ended June&nbsp;30, 2024 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Revenues for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2024 totaled $34.831&nbsp;billion, compared to $31.452&nbsp;billion in the same period of 2023. Net income attributable
to HCA Healthcare, Inc. was $3.052&nbsp;billion, or $11.47 per diluted share, compared to $2.556&nbsp;billion, or $9.14 per diluted share, for the first six months of 2023. Results for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2024 include gains on sales
of facilities of $213&nbsp;million, or $0.61 per diluted share. Results for the six months ended June&nbsp;30, 2023 included losses on sales of facilities of $14&nbsp;million, or $0.08 per diluted share. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Balance Sheet and Cash Flows from Operations </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">As of June&nbsp;30, 2024, HCA
Healthcare, Inc.&#146;s balance sheet reflected cash and cash equivalents of $831&nbsp;million, total debt of $40.880&nbsp;billion, and total assets of $57.379&nbsp;billion. During the second quarter of 2024, capital expenditures totaled
$1.281&nbsp;billion, excluding acquisitions. Cash flows provided by operating activities in the second quarter of 2024 totaled $1.971&nbsp;billion, compared to $2.475&nbsp;billion in the second quarter of 2023. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">During the second quarter of 2024, the Company repurchased 4.217&nbsp;million shares of its common stock at a cost of $1.367&nbsp;billion. The Company had
$4.228&nbsp;billion remaining under its repurchase authorization as of June&nbsp;30, 2024. As of June&nbsp;30, 2024, the Company had $7.137&nbsp;billion of availability under its credit facilities. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Dividend </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">HCA today announced that its Board of Directors declared a
quarterly cash dividend of $0.66 per share on the Company&#146;s common stock. The dividend will be paid on September&nbsp;30, 2024 to stockholders of record at the close of business on September&nbsp;16, 2024. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">The declaration and payment of any future dividend will be subject to the discretion of the Board of Directors and will depend on a variety of factors, including the
Company&#146;s financial condition, results of operations, and contractual restrictions. Future dividends are expected to be funded by cash balances and future cash flows from operations. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">2 </P>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>2024 Revised Guidance </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Today, the Company revised its 2024 estimated guidance ranges issued on January&nbsp;30, 2024. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:9pt" ALIGN="center">

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Capital expenditures for 2024, excluding acquisitions, are estimated to be in the range of $5.1 to $5.3&nbsp;billion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company&#146;s revised 2024 guidance contains a number of assumptions, including, among others, the Company&#146;s current expectations regarding patient volumes
and payor mix as well as general economic conditions, including inflation, and excludes the impact of items such as, but not limited to, gains or losses on sales of facilities, losses on retirement of debt, legal claims costs and impairment of
long-lived assets. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">Adjusted EBITDA is a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measure. A table reconciling forecasted net income attributable
to HCA Healthcare, Inc. to forecasted Adjusted EBITDA is included in this release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company&#146;s guidance is based on current plans and expectations and is
subject to a number of known and unknown uncertainties and risks, including those set forth below in the Company&#146;s &#147;Forward-Looking Statements.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Earnings Conference Call </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">HCA Healthcare will host a conference call for
investors at 9:00 a.m. Central Time today. All interested investors are invited to access a live audio broadcast of the call via webcast. The broadcast also will be available on a replay basis beginning this afternoon. The webcast can be accessed
through the Company&#146;s Investor Relations web page at
<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0000ff"><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">https://investor.hcahealthcare.com/events-and-presentations/default.aspx</FONT></FONT></U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>About the Company </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">As of
June&nbsp;30, 2024, HCA operated 188 hospitals and approximately 2,400 ambulatory sites of care, including surgery centers, freestanding emergency rooms, urgent care centers and physician clinics, in 20 states and the United Kingdom. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">This press release contains forward-looking
statements within the meaning of the federal securities laws, which involve risks and uncertainties. Forward-looking statements include the Company&#146;s financial guidance for the year ending December&nbsp;31, 2024, as well as other statements

utilize and retain qualified management and other personnel, including affiliated physicians, nurses and medical and technical support personnel, (9)&nbsp;the highly competitive nature of the health care business, (10)&nbsp;changes in service mix,

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:7.5pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">Net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc., as adjusted, diluted earnings per share, as adjusted, and Adjusted
EBITDA should not be considered as measures of financial performance under generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;). These <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures are adjusted to exclude losses (gains)
on sales of facilities and losses on retirement of debt. We believe net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc., as adjusted, diluted earnings per share, as adjusted, and Adjusted EBITDA are important measures that supplement discussions and
analysis of our results of operations. We believe it is useful to investors to provide disclosures of our results of operations on the same basis used by management. Management relies upon net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc., as
adjusted, diluted earnings per share, as adjusted, and Adjusted EBITDA as the primary measures to review and assess operating performance of its health care facilities and their management teams. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:7.5pt; font-family:ARIAL">Management and investors review both the overall performance (including net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc., as adjusted, diluted earnings
per share, as adjusted, and GAAP net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc.) and operating performance (Adjusted EBITDA) of our health care facilities. Adjusted EBITDA and the Adjusted EBITDA margin (Adjusted EBITDA divided by revenues) are
utilized by management and investors to compare our current operating results with the corresponding periods during the previous year and to compare our operating results with other companies in the health care industry. It is reasonable to expect
that adjustments, including losses (gains) on sales of facilities and losses on retirement of debt will occur in future periods, but the amounts recognized can vary significantly from period to period, do not directly relate to the ongoing
operations of our health care facilities and complicate period comparisons of our results of operations and operations comparisons with other health care companies. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:7.5pt; font-family:ARIAL">Net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc., as adjusted, diluted earnings per share, as adjusted, and Adjusted EBITDA are not measures of
financial performance under GAAP, and should not be considered as alternatives to net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc. as a measure of operating performance or cash flows from operating, investing and financing activities as a measure of
liquidity. Because net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc., as adjusted, diluted earnings per share, as adjusted, and Adjusted EBITDA are not measurements determined in accordance with GAAP and are susceptible to varying calculations, net
income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc., as adjusted, diluted earnings per share, as adjusted, and Adjusted EBITDA, as presented, may not be comparable to other similarly titled measures presented by other companies. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:11pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center">11 </P>

</DIV></Center>

losses on retirement of debt, legal claim costs (benefits) and impairments of long-lived assets because the Company does not believe that it can forecast these items with sufficient accuracy. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;). We believe Adjusted EBITDA is an important measure that supplements discussions and analysis of our results of operations. We believe it is useful to investors to provide disclosures of our results of operations on the
same basis used by management. Management relies upon Adjusted EBITDA as a primary measure to review and assess operating performance of its health care facilities and their management teams. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Management and investors review both the overall performance (including net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc.) and operating performance
(Adjusted EBITDA) of our health care facilities. Adjusted EBITDA is utilized by management and investors to compare our current operating results with the corresponding periods during the previous year and to compare our operating results with other
companies in the health care industry. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:3%; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">Adjusted EBITDA is not a measure of financial performance under GAAP and should not be considered as an
alternative to net income attributable to HCA Healthcare, Inc. as a measure of operating performance or cash flows from operating, investing and financing activities as a measure of liquidity. Because Adjusted EBITDA is not a measurement determined
in accordance with GAAP and is susceptible to varying calculations, Adjusted EBITDA, as presented, may not be comparable to other similarly titled measures presented by other companies. </P>

..report .ro, .report .rou {
	background-color: white;
}

..report .rou td {
	border-bottom: 1px solid black;
}

..report .rou table td, .report .reu table td {
	border-bottom: 0px solid black;
}

/* styles for footnote marker */
..report .fn {
	white-space: nowrap;
}

/* styles for numeric types */
..report .num, .report .nump {
	text-align: right;
	white-space: nowrap;
}

..report .nump {
	padding-left: 2em;
}

..report .nump {
	padding: 0px 0.4em 0px 2em;
}

/* styles for text types */
..report .text {
	text-align: left;
	white-space: normal;
}

..report .text .big {
	margin-bottom: 1em;
	width: 17em;
}

..report .text .more {
	display: none;
}

..report .text .note {
	font-style: italic;
	font-weight: bold;
}

	width: 10em;
}

	font-style: italic;
}

	font-size: 1em;
